py-md-3 pl-md-5 bd-conten= t" role=3D"main"> <div> =20 <div class=3D"section" id=3D"minutes-to-pandas"> <span id=3D"min"></span><h1>10 minutes to pandas<a class=3D"headerlink" hre= f=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas-docs/stable/getting_started/10min.htm= l#minutes-to-pandas" title=3D"Permalink to this headline">=C2=B6</a></h1> <p>This is a short introduction to pandas, geared mainly for new users. You can see more complex recipes in the <a class=3D"reference internal" hre= f=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas-docs/stable/user_guide/cookbook.html#= cookbook"><span class=3D"std std-ref">Cookbook</span></a>.</p> <p>Customarily, we import as follows:</p> <div class=3D"highlight-ipython notranslate"><div class=3D"highlight"><pre>= <span></span><span class=3D"gp">In [1]: </span><span class=3D"kn">import</s= pan> <span class=3D"nn">numpy</span> <span class=3D"k">as</span> <span clas= s=3D"nn">np</span> <span class=3D"gp">In [2]: </span><span class=3D"kn">import</span> <span cl= ass=3D"nn">pandas</span> <span class=3D"k">as</span> <span class=3D"nn">pd<= /span> </pre></div> </div> <div class=3D"section" id=3D"object-creation"> <h2>Object creation<a class=3D"headerlink" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.or= g/pandas-docs/stable/getting_started/10min.html#object-creation" title=3D"P= ermalink to this headline">=C2=B6</a></h2> <p>See the <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.or= g/pandas-docs/stable/getting_started/dsintro.html#dsintro"><span class=3D"s= td std-ref">Data Structure Intro section</span></a>.</p> <p>Creating a <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata= .org/pandas-docs/stable/reference/api/pandas.Series.html#pandas.Series" tit= le=3D"pandas.Series"><code class=3D"xref py py-class docutils literal notra= nslate"><span class=3D"pre">Series</span></code></a> by passing a list of v= alues, letting pandas create a default integer index:</p> <div class=3D"highlight-ipython notranslate"><div class=3D"highlight"><pre>= <span></span><span class=3D"gp">In [3]: </span><span class=3D"n">s</span> <= span class=3D"o">=3D</span> <span class=3D"n">pd</span><span class=3D"o">.<= /span><span class=3D"n">Series</span><span class=3D"p">([</span><span class= =3D"mi">1</span><span class=3D"p">,</span> <span class=3D"mi">3</span><span= class=3D"p">,</span> <span class=3D"mi">5</span><span class=3D"p">,</span>= <span class=3D"n">np</span><span class=3D"o">.</span><span class=3D"n">nan= </span><span class=3D"p">,</span> <span class=3D"mi">6</span><span class=3D= "p">,</span> <span class=3D"mi">8</span><span class=3D"p">])</span> <span class=3D"gp">In [4]: </span><span class=3D"n">s</span> <span class=3D"gh">Out[4]: </span><span class=3D"go"></span> <span class=3D"go">0 1.0</span> <span class=3D"go">1 3.0</span> <span class=3D"go">2 5.0</span> <span class=3D"go">3 NaN</span> <span class=3D"go">4 6.0</span> <span class=3D"go">5 8.0</span> <span class=3D"go">dtype: float64</span> </pre></div> </div> <p>Creating a <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata= .org/pandas-docs/stable/reference/api/pandas.DataFrame.html#pandas.DataFram= e" title=3D"pandas.DataFrame"><code class=3D"xref py py-class docutils lite= ral notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">DataFrame</span></code></a> by passing= a NumPy array, with a datetime index and labeled columns:</p> <div class=3D"highlight-ipython notranslate"><div class=3D"highlight"><pre>= <span></span><span class=3D"gp">In [5]: </span><span class=3D"n">dates</spa= n> <span class=3D"o">=3D</span> <span class=3D"n">pd</span><span class=3D"o= ">.</span><span class=3D"n">date_range</span><span class=3D"p">(</span><spa= n class=3D"s1">'20130101'</span><span class=3D"p">,</span> <span class=3D"n= ">periods</span><span class=3D"o">=3D</span><span class=3D"mi">6</span><spa= n class=3D"p">)</span> <span class=3D"gp">In [6]: </span><span class=3D"n">dates</span> <span class=3D"gh">Out[6]: </span><span class=3D"go"></span> <span class=3D"go">DatetimeIndex(['2013-01-01', '2013-01-02', '2013-01-03',= '2013-01-04',</span> <span class=3D"go"> '2013-01-05', '2013-01-06'],</span> <span class=3D"go"> dtype=3D'datetime64[ns]', freq=3D'D')</spa= n> <span class=3D"gp">In [7]: </span><span class=3D"n">df</span> <span class= =3D"o">=3D</span> <span class=3D"n">pd</span><span class=3D"o">.</span><spa= n class=3D"n">DataFrame</span><span class=3D"p">(</span><span class=3D"n">n= p</span><span class=3D"o">.</span><span class=3D"n">random</span><span clas= s=3D"o">.</span><span class=3D"n">randn</span><span class=3D"p">(</span><sp= an class=3D"mi">6</span><span class=3D"p">,</span> <span class=3D"mi">4</sp= an><span class=3D"p">),</span> <span class=3D"n">index</span><span class=3D= "o">=3D</span><span class=3D"n">dates</span><span class=3D"p">,</span> <spa= n class=3D"n">columns</span><span class=3D"o">=3D</span><span class=3D"nb">= list</span><span class=3D"p">(</span><span class=3D"s1">'ABCD'</span><span = class=3D"p">))</span> <span class=3D"gp">In [8]: </span><span class=3D"n">df</span> <span class=3D"gh">Out[8]: </span><span class=3D"go"></span> <span class=3D"go"> A B C D</span= > <span class=3D"go">2013-01-01 0.469112 -0.282863 -1.509059 -1.135632</span= > <span class=3D"go">2013-01-02 1.212112 -0.173215 0.119209 -1.044236</span= > <span class=3D"go">2013-01-03 -0.861849 -2.104569 -0.494929 1.071804</span= > <span class=3D"go">2013-01-04 0.721555 -0.706771 -1.039575 0.271860</span= > <span class=3D"go">2013-01-05 -0.424972 0.567020 0.276232 -1.087401</span= > <span class=3D"go">2013-01-06 -0.673690 0.113648 -1.478427 0.524988</span= > </pre></div> </div> <p>Creating a <code class=3D"docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"p= re">DataFrame</span></code> by passing a dict of objects that can be conver= ted to series-like.</p> <div class=3D"highlight-ipython notranslate"><div class=3D"highlight"><pre>= <span></span><span class=3D"gp">In [9]: </span><span class=3D"n">df2</span>= <span class=3D"o">=3D</span> <span class=3D"n">pd</span><span class=3D"o">= .</span><span class=3D"n">DataFrame</span><span class=3D"p">({</span><span = class=3D"s1">'A'</span><span class=3D"p">:</span> <span class=3D"mf">1.</sp= an><span class=3D"p">,</span> <span internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas= -docs/stable/reference/api/pandas.DataFrame.to_numpy.html#pandas.DataFrame.= to_numpy" title=3D"pandas.DataFrame.to_numpy"><code class=3D"xref py py-met= h docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">DataFrame.to_numpy()</s= pan></code></a> gives a NumPy representation of the underlying data. Note that this can be an expensive operation when your <a class=3D"referenc= e internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas-docs/stable/reference/= api/pandas.DataFrame.html#pandas.DataFrame" title=3D"pandas.DataFrame"><cod= e class=3D"xref py py-class docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pr= e">DataFrame</span></code></a> has columns with different data types, which comes down to a fundamental differ= ence between pandas and NumPy: <strong>NumPy arrays have one dtype for the entir= e array, while pandas DataFrames have one dtype per column</strong>. When you call <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas-do= cs/stable/reference/api/pandas.DataFrame.to_numpy.html#pandas.DataFrame.to_= numpy" title=3D"pandas.DataFrame.to_numpy"><code class=3D"xref py py-meth d= ocutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">DataFrame.to_numpy()</span= ></code></a>, pandas will find the NumPy dtype that can hold <em>all</em> of the dtypes in the DataFrame. This may end up being <code class=3D"docuti= ls literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">object</span></code>, which req= uires casting every value to a Python object.</p> <p>For <code class=3D"docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">df<= /span></code>, our <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"https://pandas.p= ydata.org/pandas-docs/stable/reference/api/pandas.DataFrame.html#pandas.Dat= aFrame" title=3D"pandas.DataFrame"><code class=3D"xref py py-class docutils= literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">DataFrame</span></code></a> of al= l floating-point values, <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas-do= cs/stable/reference/api/pandas.DataFrame.to_numpy.html#pandas.DataFrame.to_= numpy" title=3D"pandas.DataFrame.to_numpy"><code class=3D"xref py py-meth d= ocutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">DataFrame.to_numpy()</span= ></code></a> is fast and doesn=E2=80=99t require copying data.</p> <div class=3D"highlight-ipython notranslate"><div class=3D"highlight"><pre>= <span></span><span class=3D"gp">In [17]: </span><span class=3D"n">df</span>= <span class=3D"o">.</span><span class=3D"n">to_numpy</span><span class=3D"p= ">()</span> <span class=3D"gh">Out[17]: </div> </div> <div class=3D"section" id=3D"selection"> <h2>Selection<a class=3D"headerlink" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pand= as-docs/stable/getting_started/10min.html#selection" title=3D"Permalink to = this headline">=C2=B6</a></h2> <div class=3D"alert alert-info"> <p class=3D"admonition-title">Note</p> <p>While standard Python / Numpy expressions for selecting and setting are intuitive and come in handy for interactive work, for production code, we recommend the optimized pandas data access methods, <code class=3D"docutils= literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">.at</span></code>, <code class=3D= "docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">.iat</span></code>, <code class=3D"docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">.loc</span= ></code> and <code class=3D"docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"pr= e">.iloc</span></code>.</p> </div> <p>See the indexing documentation <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"h= ttps://pandas.pydata.org/pandas-docs/stable/user_guide/indexing.html#indexi= ng"><span class=3D"std std-ref">Indexing and Selecting Data</span></a> and = <a class=3D"reference internal" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas-do= cs/stable/user_guide/advanced.html#advanced"><span class=3D"std std-ref">Mu= ltiIndex / Advanced Indexing</span></a>.</p> <div class=3D"section" id=3D"getting"> <h3>Getting<a class=3D"headerlink" href=3D"https://pandas.pydata.org/pandas= -docs/stable/getting_started/10min.html#getting" title=3D"Permalink to this= headline">=C2=B6</a></h3> <p>Selecting a single column, which yields a <code class=3D"docutils litera= l notranslate"><span class=3D"pre">Series</span></code>, equivalent to <code class=3D"docutils literal notranslate"><span class=3D"p= re">df.A</span></code>:</p> <div class=3D"highlight-ipython notranslate"><div class=3D"highlight"><pre>= <span></span><span class=3D"gp">In [23]: </span><span class=3D"n">df</span>= <span class=3D"p">[</span><span class=3D"s1">'A'</span><span class=3D"p">]<= /span> <span class=3D"gh">Out[23]: </span><span class=3D"go"></span> <span class=3D"go">2013-01-01 0.469112</span> <span class=3D"go">2013-01-02 1.212112</span> <span class=3D"go">2013-01-03 -0.861849</span> <span class=3D"go">2013-01-04 0.721555</span> <span class=3D"go">2013-01-05 -0.424972</span> <span
